)@@G@@D TO SEE IF THEY ARE LEGAL    GPQ12300    @I@@@@GPX$ALLQ* J         $-$ DR
)@@G@@                .                               GPQ12400    @I@@@@      DS
)@@G@@    SLJ      GPX$K              . GET THE VALUE OF THE QUEUE NO.  GPQ125DT

)@@G@@ SO THEN ERROR                GPQ12700    @I@@@@          TLE,U    A1,1 DW
)@@G@@              . SEE IF SMALLER THAN 1           GPQ12800    @I@@@@      DX
)@@G@@    J        GPX$QSIZE          . IF TRUE THEN ERROR              GPQ129DY
)@@G@@00    @I@@@@          L,U       A2,GPXQ$            . PICK UP ADDRESS OFDZ
)@@G@@ QUEUEQ     GPQ13000    @I@@@@          SLJ      GPX$ENTITY         . GOEA
)@@G@@ SEE IF THIS QUE EXISTS       GPQ13100    @I@@@@          J        GPX$AEB
)@@G@@LLQ           .                                 GPQ13200    @I@@@@. GET EC
)@@G@@THE CURRENT SIZE OF THE QUEUE                                     GPQ133ED
)@@G@@00    @I@@@@GPX$Q*    J        $-$                .                     EE
)@@G@@            GPQ13400    @I@@@@          SLJ      GPX$ALLQ           . GEEF
)@@G@@T THE ADDRESS OF THE QUE      GPQ13500    @I@@@@          L,U      A1,0 EG
)@@G@@              . SET FOR ERROR                   GPQ13600    @I@@@@      EH
)@@G@@    JN       A2,*GPX$Q          . RETURN FOR NON-EXISTANCE        GPQ137EI
)@@G@@00    @I@@@@          L        A1,6,A2            . PICK UP THE CURRENT EJ
)@@G@@COUNT       GPQ13800    @I@@@@          J         *GPX$Q            . REEK
)@@G@@TURN                          GPQ13900    @I@@@@. THIS PICKS UP THE MAXIEL
)@@G@@MUM COUNT AT ANY ONE TIME                       GPQ14000    @I@@@@GPX$QMEM
)@@G@@*   J        $-$                .                                 GPQ141EN
)@@G@@00    @I@@@@          SLJ      GPX$ALLQ           . GET QUEUE ADDRESS   EO
)@@G@@            GPQ14200    @I@@@@          L,U      A1,0               . LOEP
)@@G@@AD FOR ERROR                  GPQ14300    @I@@@@          JN       A2,*GEQ

)@@G@@    L        A1,7,A2            . GET THE MAX. COUNT              GPQ145ES

)@@G@@E QUEUE                       GPQ14700    @I@@@@GPX$QA*   J         $-$ EV

)@@G@@            GPQ15000    @I@@@@          JN        A2,*GPX$QA        . REEZ

)@@G@@     . QW-IO@H@@@@. NEEDED BY THE USER.                                 FU

)@@G@@                             . QW-IO@H@@@@-795                          FW
)@@G@@                                         . QW-IO@H@@@@          L       FX

)@@G@@@H@@@@          J         NORM60            . NO, SKIP                  GA

)@@G@@RDS  . QW-OT@H@@@@          LMJ       X11,RSCONV        . NO, USE RSI COHD

)@@G@@     . QW-OT@H@@@@          S         A0,R2             . SAVE PACKET ADHK

)@@G@@A0      . RESET CHARACTER COUNT          . QW-OT@H@@@@          L,U     HU
)@@G@@  A2,FMC060         . GET ADDRESS OF STORE CO-ROUTINE. QW-OT@H@@@@      HV
)@@G@@    L         A4,D5UMBT,A3      . GET UOM BITS                   . QW-OTHW

)@@G@@                 . QW-OT@H@@@@          L,U       A5,CR             . YEHZ

)@@G@@        . GET FLAG (077) AND IGNORE      . QW-OT@H@@@@FMC020    JGD     II

)@@G@@    L         A0,R2             . RESTORE PACKET ADDRESS         . QW-OTIK
)@@G@@@H@@@@          J         NORM90            . ALL DONE EXIT             IL

)@@G@@END 8 BITS OTHERWISE         . QW-OT@H@@@@. FORCE EVEN PARITY AND STORE IO
)@@G@@IN HALF WORDS                            . QW-OT@H@@@@.                 IP
)@@G@@                                                     . QW-OT@H@@@@FMC030IQ

)@@G@@ FOR CBLOX  @[@@@@-18,18@G@@@@.       S2 OF DESCRIPTOR INDICATES ONE OF II
)@@G@@THE FOLLOWING DATA MODES.     @F@@@@.       SOME OF THE MODE VALUES BELOIJ
)@@G@@W ARE USED AS FLAGS AND DO NOT@G@@@@.       APPEAR IN ACTUAL DATA IN THEIK

)@@G@@ TO THE PROCESSOR.@[@@@@.     @[@@@@-24,24@G@@@@ZMOIND  EQU    5        IM
)@@G@@      . STASH FLAG.  INDICATES THAT THE RESULT  @G@@@@                  IN
)@@G@@            . OF A FUNC IS INDEFINITE, I.E. IS INTEGER@G@@@@            IO
)@@G@@                  . WHICH MAY EXCEED 17 BITS (REQUIRING     @G@@@@      IP
)@@G@@                        . CONVERSION OF PREVIOUSLY CALCULATED     @E@@@@IQ
)@@G@@                              . RESULTS TO DFLOAT)     .    @[@@@@-26,27IR
)@@G@@@G@@@@ZMODFI  EQU    8              . FETCH FLAG. INDICATES THAT A DFLOAIS
)@@G@@T     @G@@@@                              . OPERAND MUST BE CONVERTED TOIT
)@@G@@ HALFINT (BY@G@@@@                              . TAKING THE FLOOR) AS IIU
)@@G@@T IS BEING FETCHED@G@@@@ZMOIDF  EQU    5              . FETCH FLAG.  INDIV
)@@G@@ICATES THAT A HALFINT   @G@@@@                              . OPERAND ISIW
)@@G@@ TO BE FLOATED AS IT IS BEING @G@@@@                              . FETCIX
)@@G@@HED.  NOTE: WHEN ALL REFS IN THE    @G@@@@                              IY
)@@G@@. PROCESSOR TO THE TAG 'ZMOINT' HAVE BEEN @G@@@@                        IZ
)@@G@@      . REMOVED, THE VALUE OF ZMOIDF WILL BE    @C@@@@                  JA
)@@G@@            . CHANGED TO 9    @B@@@@*CONFIG . PERMANENT CORRECTIONS FOR JB
